return slide\r\n\r\n# Helper to add content slide with title and body\r\ndef add_content_slide(title, bullets):\r\n    slide_layout = prs.slide_layouts[1]  # Title and Content\r\n    slide = prs.slides.add_slide(slide_layout)\r\n    slide.shapes.title.text = title\r\n    tf = slide.placeholders[1].text_frame\r\n    tf.clear()\r\n    for i, b in enumerate(bullets):\r\n        if i == 0:\r\n            p = tf.paragraphs[0]\r\n        else:\r\n            p = tf.add_paragraph()\r\n        p.text = b\r\n        p.level = 0 if i == 0 else 1\r\n    return slide\r\n\r\n# Helper to add two-content slide\r\ndef add_two_content_slide(title, left_items, right_items):\r\n    slide_layout = prs.slide_layouts[3]  # Two Content\r\n    slide = prs.slides.add_slide(slide_layout)\r\n    slide.shapes.title.text = title\r\n    left_tf = slide.placeholders[1].text_frame\r\n    left_tf.clear()\r\n    for i, txt in enumerate(left_items):\r\n        p = left_tf.paragraphs[0] if i == 0 else left_tf.add_paragraph()\r\n        p.text = txt\r\n        p.level = 0 if i == 0 else 1\r\n    right_tf = slide.placeholders[2].text_frame\r\n    right_tf.clear()\r\n    for i, txt in enumerate(right_items):\r\n        p = right_tf.paragraphs[0] if i == 0 else right_tf.add_paragraph()\r\n        p.text = txt\r\n        p.level = 0 if i == 0 else 1\r\n    return slide\r\n\r\n# Helper to add blank slide with placeholders boxes\r\ndef add_chart_placeholder_slide(title, notes):\r\n    slide_layout = prs.slide_layouts[6]  # Blank\r\n    slide = prs.slides.add_slide(slide_layout)\r\n    # Title textbox\r\n    title_box = slide.shapes.add_textbox(Inches(0.5), Inches(0.2), Inches(12), Inches(0.6))\r\n    title_tf = title_box.text_frame\r\n    title_run = title_tf.paragraphs[0].add_run()\r\n    title_run.text = title\r\n    title_run.font.size = Pt(32)\r\n    title_run.font.bold = True\r\n    # Three chart placeholders\r\n    w = Inches(3.8); h = Inches(3.0)\r\n    x_positions = [Inches(0.5), Inches(4.45), Inches(8.4)]\r\n    for i, x in enumerate(x_positions):\r\n        shape = slide.shapes.add_shape(MSO_SHAPE.RECTANGLE, x, Inches(1.2), w, h)\r\n        fill = shape.fill\r\n        fill.solid()\r\n        fill.fore_color.theme_color = MSO_THEME_COLOR.ACCENT_1\r\n        fill.transparency = 0.85\r\n        shape.line.color.theme_color = MSO_THEME_COLOR.ACCENT_1\r\n        tf = shape.text_frame\r\n        tf.text = f\"ì°¨íŠ¸ ìë¦¬ #{i+1}\"\r\n        tf.paragraphs[0].alignment = PP_ALIGN.CENTER\r\n    # Notes area\r\n    notes_box = slide.shapes.add_textbox(Inches(0.5), Inches(4.4), Inches(12.3), Inches(2))\r\n    notes_tf = notes_box.text_frame\r\n    notes_tf.text = notes\r\n    return slide\r\n\r\n# 1) Cover\r\nadd_title_slide(\"ê¸°ì—… ë³´ê³ ì„œ + ì°¨íŠ¸ ê¸°ë°˜ ë§¤ë§¤ì „ëµ\", \"ê¸°ì—…ëª… / ë¶„ì„ì¼ì / ì• ë„ë¦¬ìŠ¤íŠ¸\")\r\n\r\n# 2) ëª©ì°¨\r\nadd_content_slide(\"ëª©ì°¨\", [\r\n
